1a1(mdo 'grel): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i mnangag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan zhes bya ba rje btsun byams pa mgon pos mdzad pa bzhugs/
1b1(mdo 'grel): rgya gar skad du/ a b+hi sa ma yA lang+ga ra nA ma
1b2(mdo 'grel): prad+d+hA p+tA ma ti dan/ 'ongs
2a1(mdo 'grel): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan zhes bya ba'i tshig le'ur byas
2a2(mdo 'grel): pa/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// nyan thos zhi ba tshol rnams kun shes nyid kyis
2a3(mdo 'grel): nyer zhing khrid mdzad gang yin dang // 'gro la phan par byed rnams lam shes nyid kyis 'jig rten don sgrub mdzad pa gang //
2b1(mdo 'grel): gang dang yang dag ldan pas thub rnams rnam pa kun ldan sna tshogs 'di gsungs pa// nyan thos byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs bcas sangs rgyas kyi ni yum de la phyag 'tshal// rnaM pa
2b2(mdo 'grel): thams cad mkhyen nyid lam// ston pas 'di las bshad pa gang // gzhan gyis myong ba ma yin te// chos spyod bcu yi bdag nyid kyi// mdo don dran pa la bzhag nas// blo dang ldan pas
2b3(mdo 'grel): mthong 'gyur phyir// bde blag tu ni rtogs pa zhes// bya ba rtsom pa'i dgos pa yin// shes rab pha rol phyin pa ni// dngos po brgyad kyis yang dag bshad// rnam kun mkhyen nyid lam
2b4(mdo 'grel): shes nyid// de nas thams cad shes pa nyid// rnam kun mngon rdzogs rtogs pa dang // rtse mor phyin dang mthar gyis pa// skad cig gcig mngon rdzogs byang chub// chos kyi sku dang de rnam brgyad//
3a1(mdo 'grel): sems bskyod pa dang gdams ngag dang // ngos 'byod yan lag rnam bzhi dang // sgrub pa yi ni rten gyur pa// chos kyi dbyings kyi rang bzhin dang // dmigs pa dag dang chod dang ni// go cha 'jug pa'i bya ba dang //
3a2(mdo 'grel): tshogs ni nges par 'byung bcas rnams// thub pa'i rnam kun mkhyen pa nyid// mog mog por byed la sogs dang // slob ma bse ru'i lam gang dang // 'di dang gzhan pa'i yon tan gyis// phan yon che ba mthong ba'i lam//
3a3(mdo 'grel): byed pa dang ni mos pa dang // bstod dang bkur dang bsngags pa dang // bsngo dang rjes su yi rang po// yid la byed pa bla med dag/ sgrub dang shin tu dag pa zhes// bya ba 'dri ni sgom pa'i lam// byang chub sems dpa' mkhas rnams
3a4(mdo 'grel): kyi// lam shes nyid ni de 'drar bshad// shes pas srid pa mi gnas shing // snying rjes zhi la mi gnas dang // thabs ma yin pas ring ba dang // thabs kyis ring ba ma yin nyid// mi mthun gnyen po'i phyogs dag dang // sbyor dang
3a5(mdo 'grel): de yi mnyam nyid dang // nyan thos la sogs mthong ba'i lam// de 'dra kun shes nyid du 'dod// rnam pa sbyor bar bcas rnams dang // yon tan skyon ni mtshan nyid bcas// thar dang nges 'byed cha mthun dang // slob pa phyir mi ldog
3a6(mdo 'grel): pa'i tshogs// srid dang zhi ba mnyam nyid dang // zhing dag bla na med pa ni// rnam kun mngon rdzogs rtogs pa ste// 'di ni thabs mkhas bcas pa yin// de yi rtags dang rnam 'phel dang // brtan dang sems kun gnas pa dang //
3b1(mdo 'grel): mthong nas bya dang sbrum pa zhes// bya ba'o lam na so so la// rnam par rtog pa rnam bzla sa// gnyen po rnam pa bzhi dang ni// bar chad med pa'i ting nge 'dzin// log par bsgrub dang bcas pa ni// rtse ma'i mngon rtogs mthar gyos pa// rnam gas/
3b2(mdo 'grel): rnam bcu skad cig ma// gcig gis mngon rdzogs byang chub pa// mtshan nyid kyis ni rnam pa bzhi// ngo bo nyid longs rdzogs bcas dang // de bzhin gzhan pa sprul pa ni// chos sku mdzad pa dang bcas pa// rnam pa bzhir ni yang dag brjod//
3b3(mdo 'grel): sems bskyed pa ni gzhan don phyir// yang dag rdzogs pa'i byang chub 'dod// de dang de ni mdo bzhin du// bsdus dang rgyas pa'i sgo nas brjod// de yang sa gser zla ba me// gtar dang rin chen 'byung gnas mtsho// rdo rje ri sman bshes
3b4(mdo 'grel): gnyen dang // yid bzhin nor bu nyi la glu// rgyal po mdzod dang lam po che// bzhon pa bkod ma'i chu dang ni// sgra snyan chu bo sprin rnams kyis// rnam pa nyi shu rtsa gnyis so// sgrub dang bden pa rnams dang ni// sangs rgyas la sogs dkon
3b5(mdo 'grel): mchog gsum// ma zhen yongs su mi ngal dang // lam ni yongs su 'dzin pa dang // spyan lnga dang ni mngon shes kyi// yon tan drug dang mthong lam dang // sgrom zhes bya la gdams ngag ni// bcu yi bdag nyid shes par bya// dbang po rtul
3b6(mdo 'grel): dang rnon po dag/ dad dang mthong thob rigs nas rigs// bar chad gcig par skyes nas dang // byed dang byed min 'og min 'gro// 'phar gsum srid rtse'i mthar thug 'gro// gzugs kyi chags bcom mthong ba yi// chos la zhi lus
4a1(mdo 'grel): mngon sum byed// bso r+ya dang ni nyi shu'o// dmigs pa dang ni rnam pa dang // rgyu dang yongs su 'dzin pa dang // byang chub sems dpa' skyob pa yi// drod sogs bdag nyid ji bzhin du// rnam rtog bzhi po ldan bston
4a2(mdo 'grel): ba// chung dang 'bring dang chen po rnams// nyan thos bse ru lta bu dang // bcas pa dag las khyad par bapags// dmigs pa mi rtag la sogs pa// bden pa'i rten can de yi ni// rnam pa mngon zhan la sogs 'gog+sa/ rig pa gsum tsa
4a3(mdo 'grel): 'thob pa'i rgyu// gzugs sogs 'du 'god gnas bral dang // gnas dang btags dang brjod du med// gzugs sogs mi gnas de dag ni// de yi ngo bo rang bzhin med// de dag gcig gi rang bzhin gcig/ de mi rtags sogs par mi
4a4(mdo 'grel): gnas// de rnams de yi ngo bas sbyong // de dag gcig gi rang bzhin gcig/ chos rnams mi 'dzin gang yin dang // de dag mtshan mar mi mthong phyir// shes rab kyis ni yongs rtog pa// thams cad dmigs su med par ro// gzugs
4a5(mdo 'grel): sogs ngo bo nyid med nyid// de med pa nyid ngo bo nyid// de dag skye med nges 'byung med// ngag dang de dag mtshan ma med// de yi mtshan mar mi brten pas// mos min 'du shes med pa yin// ting 'dzin de yi byed pa nyid// lung ston pa dang /
4a6(mdo 'grel): rlom pa zad// gsum po phan tshun ngo bo gcig/ ting 'dzin rnam par mi rtag pa// de ltar nges 'byes cha mthun ni// chung dang 'bring dang chen po yin// gzhi dang de yi gnyen po yis// gzung bar rtog pa rnam pa gnyis// rmongs dang du
4b1(mdo 'grel): sogs bye brag gis// don so sor rnam pa dgu// rdzus dang btags pa'i rten can gyis// 'dzin pa'ang rnam pa gnyis su 'dod// rang dbang bdag sogs ngo bo dang // phung sogs rten las de bzhin no// sems mi 'gong pa nyid la sogs// /
4b2(mdo 'grel): ngo bo nyid med sogs ston byed// de yi mi mthun phyogs bor bu// rnam pa kun tu yongs 'dzin yin// rtogs pa yi ni chos drug dang // gnyen po dang ni spong ba dang // de dag yongs su gtugs pa dang // shes rab snying brtser bcas pa dang // slob
4b3(mdo 'grel): ma thun mang min nyid dang // gzhan gyi don gyi go rim dang // ye shes rtsol ba mi mnga' bar// 'jug pa'i rten la rigs zhes bya// chos kyi dbyings la dbyer med phyir// rigs ni tha dad rung ma yin// brten pa'i chos kyi bye brag gis// de yi dbye
4b4(mdo 'grel): ba yongs su brjod// dmigs pa chos rnams thams cad de// de yang dge la sogs pa yin// 'jig rten pa yi rtogs pa dang // gang dag 'jig rten 'das 'dod dang // zag bcas zag pa med chos dang // gang dag 'dus byas 'dus ma byas//
4b5(mdo 'grel): slob ma thun mong chos rnams dang // gang dag thub pa'i thun mong min// sems can kun mchog nyid sems dang // spong dang rtogs dang gsum po la// chen po gsum po rang byung gi/ ched du bya ba 'di shes bya// de dag so sor sbyin la sogs//
4b6(mdo 'grel): rnam pa drug tu bsdus pa yis// cho ga'i sgrub pa gang yin de// drug tshan drug gis ji bzhin bshad// bsam gtan gzugs med sbyin sogs dang // lam dang byams la sogs pa dang // dmigs pa med dang ldan pa dang // 'khor
5a1(mdo 'grel): gsum rnam par dag pa dang // ched du bya dang mngon shes drug/ rnam kun mkhyen pa'i tshul la ni// 'jug pa'i sgrub pa theg chen la// 'dzeg pa yin par shes par bya// brtse dang sbyin la sogs pa drug/ zhi gnas
5a2(mdo 'grel): lhag mthong bcas pa dang // zung du 'brel pa'i lam gang dang // thabs la mkhas pa gang yin dang // ye shes dang ni bsod nams dang // lam dang gzung dang sa bcu dang // gnyen po'i tshogs kyi skyob pa yi// rim pa yin par shes
5a3(mdo 'grel): bar bya// yongs su sbyong ba rnam bcu yis// sa ni dang po 'thob 'gyur te// bsam dang phan pa'i dngos nyid dang // sems can rnams la sems mnyam nyid// gtong dang bshes gnyen bsten pa dang // dam chos dmigs pa tshol ba
5a4(mdo 'grel): dang // rtag tu nges 'byung sems nyid dang // sangs rgyas bkur 'dod dga' ba dang // chos ston pa dang bden pa yi// tshig ni bcu pa yin par 'dod// 'di dag rang bzhin mi dmigs pas// yongs su sbyong bar shes par bya// tshul
5a5(mdo 'grel): khrims byas pa gzo dang bzod// rab tu dga' dang snying brtse che// bkur sti bla ma la gus nyan// brgyad pa sbyin pa sogs la brtson// thos pas mi ngoms nyid dang ni// zang zing med par chos sbyin dang // sangs rgyas zhing kun sbyor
5a6(mdo 'grel): ba dang // 'khor bas yongs su mi skyo dang // ngo tsha khrel yod ces bya ba// rlom med bdag nyid de rnam lnga// nags gnas 'dod chung chog shes dang // sbyangs pa yang dag sdom sten dang // bslab pa yongs su mi gtong dang // 'dod pa rnams
5b1(mdo 'grel): la smod pa dang // mya ngan 'das dang bdog kun gtong // mi zhum pa dang lta ba med// 'dris dang khyim la 'khren pa dang // 'du 'dzir gyur pa'i gnas dang ni// bdag bstod gzhan la brnyas pa dang // mi dge'i las kyi lam bcu dang //
5b2(mdo 'grel): rlom pas khengs dang phyin ci log/ blo ngan dang nyon mongs bzod// bcu po 'di ni rnam spangs nas// sa lnga pa ni yang dag 'thob// sbyin dang tshul khrims bzod brtson 'grus// bsam gtan shes rab rab rdzogs pas// slob ma dang ni bse
5b3(mdo 'grel): ru la// dga' dang skrag pa'i sems spangs pa// bslangs na mi zhum bdog pa kun// btang yang mi dga' med pa dang // dbul yang slong ba mi spong bas// sa ni drug pa yang dag 'thob// bdag dang sems can 'dzin pa dang // srog dang gang
5b4(mdo 'grel): zag chad rtag dang // mtshan ma rgyu dang phung po dang // khams dang skye mched dag dang ni// khams gsum pa la gnas dang chags// sems ni kun tu zhum pa dang // dkon mchog gsum dang tshul khrims la// der lta ba yi mngon zhen dang //
5b5(mdo 'grel): stong pa nyid la rtsod pa dang // de dang 'gal ba'i nyes pa ni// nyi shu gang la rnam chad pa// de yis sa ni bdun pa 'thob// rnam thar sgo gsum shes pa dang // 'khor gsum rnam par dag nyid dang // snying rje dang ni rlom med dang // chos mnyam
5b6(mdo 'grel): nyid dang tshul gcig shes// mi skye ba dang bzod shes dang // chos rnams rnam pa gcig tu ston// rtog pa kun tu 'joms pa dang // 'du shes lha dang nyon mongs spong // zhi gnas nges par sems pa dang // lhag mthong la ni mkhas pa
6a1(mdo 'grel): dang // sems dul ba dang thams cad la// thogs pa med pa'i ye shes dang // chags pa'i sa min gar 'dod par// zhing gzhan du ni mnyam 'gro dang // kun tu bdag gi ngo bo ni// ston pa nyid dang nyi shu'o// sems
6a2(mdo 'grel): can kun yid shes pa dang // mngon par shes pas brtse ba dang // sangs rgyas zhing bzang bsgrub pa dang // yongs su brtag phyir sangs rgyas bsten// dpa' bo shes dang rgyal ba yi// zhing skyong sgyu ma ltar gnas dang // bsams bzhin
6a3(mdo 'grel): sred pa len pa dang // las ni rnam pa 'di brgyad bshad// smon lam dag ni mtha' yas dang // lha la sogs pa'i skad shes dang // spobs pa chu bo lta bu dang // mngal du 'jug pa mchog dang ni// rigs dang rus dang cho 'brang dang // 'khor
6a4(mdo 'grel): dang skye ba dag dang ni// nges 'byung byang chub shing rnams dang // yon tan phun sum tshogs pa yin// sa dang 'das nas ye shes ni// gang gis sangs rgyas sar gnas pa// de ni byang chub sems dpa'i sa// bcu pa yin par shes par
6a5(mdo 'grel): bya// mthong dang goms pa'i lam dag la// gzung dang 'dzin pa'i rnam rtog rnams// nye bar zhi bar bya ba'i phyir// gnyen po rnam pa brgyad ces bya// ched du bya dang mnyam nyid dang // sems can don dang 'bad med dang // mtha' las
6a6(mdo 'grel): 'das par nges 'byung dang // thob pa'i mtshan nyid nges 'byung dang // rnam pa thams cad mkhyen nyid dang // lam gyi yul can nges 'byung ste// rnam pa brgyad kyi bdag nyid 'di// nges pabyung sgrub pa yin zhes bya// shes rab kyi pha rol tu
6b1(mdo 'grel): phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi tshig le'ur byas pa las/ skabs dang po'o// / lha rnams rung bar bya ba'i phyir// 'od kyis mog mog por mdzad dang // yul nges pa dang khyab pa dang // 8nga
6b2(mdo 'grel): bzhin dang ni de yi las// lam shes nyid kyi tshul la ni// 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi dag gi/ rnam pa mi dmigs sgo nas ni// nyan thos lam 'di shes par bya// 'phags pa nyan thos lam la ni// gzugs la sogs pa stong pa'i phyir// stong
6b3(mdo 'grel): pa nyid rnams dbyer med pas// dro ba de dag mi dmigs pas// rtse mor gyur pa dag tu 'dod// de la rtag la sogs tshul gyis// gnas pa bkag pas bzod pa rnams// sa bcu dag las brtsams nas ni// mi gnas rgyas par bstan pa
6b4(mdo 'grel): yis// chos kyi mchog tu 'gyur bshad de// ci phyir zhe na sangs rgyas kyis// mkhyen nas chos rnams ma gzigs phyir// rang byung bdag nyid rtogs pa'i phyir// gzhan gyis bstan yang mi dgos la// bse ru lta bu'i ye shes ni// zab pa nyid
6b5(mdo 'grel): du mngon par brjod// gang gang don ni gang gang la// ji lta ji ltar nyan 'dod pa// de de la don de dang de// sgra med kyang de de ltar snang // gzung don rtog pa spong phyir dang // 'dzin pa mi spong phyir dang ni// rten gyis bse ru lta bu'i lam// yang
6b6(mdo 'grel): dag bsdus par shes par bya// btags pa'i chos nyid mi 'gal bar// ston pa'i rnam pa dror gyur pa// rtse mor gyur pa gzugs la sogs// 'grib pa meng la sogs pas phye// nang stong nyid la sogs pa yis// gzugs sogs
7a1(mdo 'grel): mi 'dzin phyir bzod pa// gzugs sogs skye ba med sogs kyi// rnam pa can ni chos kyi mchog/ bden dang bden la bzod pa dang // shes pa'i skad cig rnam bzhi yis// lam shes nyid la mthong ba'i lam// phan yon
7a2(mdo 'grel): bcas pa 'di bshad do// de bzhin nyid dang sangs rgyas dag/ phan tshun brten pa rten med phyir// rnam grangs khas mi len pa dang // chen po tshad ma med bcas dang // tshad med pa dang mtha' med dang // der gnas gzugs la sogs
7a3(mdo 'grel): // sangs rgyas nyid du nges 'dzin dang // blang med dor ba med sogs dang // byams la sogs dang stong nyid dang // sangs rgyas nyid ni 'thob pa dang // rnam par byang kun yongs bsdus dang // nyam nga ba dang nad kun sel// mya ngan
7a4(mdo 'grel): 'das 'dzin zhi nyid dang // sangs rgyas rnams kyis bsrung la sogs// srog mi gcod pa la sogs pa// rnam pa kun mkhyen tshul la ni// bdag nyid gnas te sems can dag/ 'god dang sbyin pa la sogs pa// rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu
7a5(mdo 'grel): bsngo ba// lam shes nyid kyi skad cig ma// kun nas zhi dang thams cad la// bdud dang nyon mongs las rgyal dang // gnod pas brdzi ba med nyid dang // byang chub dang ni rten mchod nyid// mos pa rang gi don dang ni// rang gzhan don dang gzhan
7a6(mdo 'grel): don dang // rnam gsum shes bya de yang ni// chung dang 'bring dang chen po ste// so sor rnam pa gsum du 'dod// chung ngu'i chung sogs dbye ba yis// de yang rnam gsum de ltar na// rnam pa nyi shu bdun du 'dod// shes rab pha rol phyin pa
7b1(mdo 'grel): pa la// mos pa'i gnas skabs rnams la ni// dgu tshan gsum gyis bstod pa dang // bkur ba dang ni bsngags par 'dod// yongs su bsngo ba khyad par can// de yi byed pa mchog yin no// de ni dmigs med rnam pa can// phyin ci
7b2(mdo 'grel): ma log mtshan nyid do// dben dang sangs rgyas bsod nams tshogs// rang bzhin dran pa'i spyod yul can// thabs bcas mtshan ma med pa dang // sangs rgyas rjesu yi rang dang // khams gsum gtogs pa ma yin dang // chung dang badri
7b3(mdo 'grel): dradrang chen po yi// bsngo ba gzhan ni rnam gsum po// bsod nams chu 'byung bdag nyid do// thabs dang mi dmigs pa dag gis// dge ba'i rtsa la yi rang ba// rje su yi rang yid byed pa// sgom pa yin par 'dir brjod do// de yi ngo
7b4(mdo 'grel): nyid mchog nyid// kun la mngon par 'du mi byed// chos rnams dmigs med par ni// gtod par byed pa don chen nyid// sangs rgyas bsnyen dang sbyin sogs dang // thabs la mkhas pa gang yin pa// 'di la mos pa'i rgyu dag yin//
7b5(mdo 'grel): chos kyi phongs pa'i rgyu dag ni// bdud kyi thibs kyis non pa dang // zab mo'i chos la ma myos dang // phung po la sogs mngon zhen dang // sdig pa'i grogs pos yongs zin pa'o// 'bras bu dag pa gzugs la sogs// dag pa nyid de
7b6(mdo 'grel): gang gi phyir// de gnyis tha dad ma yin zhing // bcad du med pas dag par brjod// nyon mongs shes bya lam gsum gyi// nyams phyir slob ma bse ru dang // rgyal sras rnams kyi dag pa ste// sangs rgyas rnam kun shin tu ga/
8a1(mdo 'grel): sa dgu la ni chen po yi// chen po la sogs dri ma yi// gAnyen po chung ngu'i chung ngu la// sogs pa'i lam ni dag pa yin// de la klan ka spangs pa yis// lam ni 'jal dang gzhal bya dag/ mnyam pa nyid kyis
8a2(mdo 'grel): khams gsum gyi// gnyen po nyid du 'dod pa yin// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi tshig le'ur byas pa las/ skabs gnyis pa'o// // tshu rel pha rol mtha' la
8a3(mdo 'grel): min// de dag par na mi gnas pa// dus rnams mnyam pa nyid shes phyir// shes rab pha rol phyin par 'dod// de ni mtshan mar dmigs sgo nas// thabs ma yin pas ring bas te// de ni thabs la mkhas pa yis// yang dag nye ba
8a4(mdo 'grel): nyid du bshad// gzugs sogs phung po stong nyid dang // dus gsum gtogs pa'i chos rnams dang // sbyin sogs byang chub phyogs rnams la// spyod pa'i 'du shes mi mthun phyogs// sbyin la sogs la ngar 'dzin med// gzhan
8a5(mdo 'grel): dag de la sbyor byed pa// de ni chags pa'i mtha' 'gog pas// rgyal la sogs la chags pa phra// chos kyi lam ni rang bzhin gyis// dben pa'i phyir na de zab nyid// chos rnams rang bzhin gcig par ni// shes pas chags pa sdong ba
8a6(mdo 'grel): yin// mthong ba la sogs bkag pa yis// de ni rtogs par dka' bar bshad// gzugs la sogs par mi shes phyir// de ni bsam mi khyab par 'dod// de ltar kun shes nyid lugs la// mi mthun gnyen po'i phyogs dag gi//

9a1(mdo 'grel): byas pa las/ skabs gsum pa// // gni shes pa yi bye brag rnams// rnam pa zhes bya mtshan nyid de// kun mkhyen nyid ni rnam gsum phyir// de ni rnam pa gsum du 'dod// med pa'i rnam pa nas bzung ste/
9a2(mdo 'grel): mi g.yo ba yi rnam pa'i bar// bden pa so so la bzhi dang // lam la de ni bco lngar bshad// rgyu dang lam dang sdug bsngal dang // 'gog pa la ni go rim bzhin// de dag brgyad dang bdun dang ni// lnga dang bcu drug ces bsgrags so// dran
9a3(mdo 'grel): pa nyer gzhag nas gzung ste// sangs rgyas rnam pa'i mthar thug rnams// lam gyi bden pa'i rjes mthun par// kun mkhyen gsum du phye bas na// slob ma byang chub sems dpa' dang // sangs rgyas rnams la rim bzhin de// sum cu
9a4(mdo 'grel): bdun dang sum cu bzhi// sum cu rtsa dgu dag tu bzhed// sangs rgyas rnams la lhag par byas// de la dge ba'i rtsa ba bskrun// dge ba'i bshes kyi mgon bcas pa// 'di mnyan pa yi snod yin no// sangs rgyas bsten dang kun 'dri dang /
9a5(mdo 'grel): sbyin dang tshul khrims sogs spyod pas// len dang 'dzin pa la sogs pa'i// snod du dam pa rnams bzhed do// gzugs la sogs la mi gnas phyir// de la sbyor ba bkag pa'i phyir// de yi de bzhin nyid zab phyir// de rnams gting
9a6(mdo 'grel): dpag dka' ba'i phyir// de dag tshad ni med phyir dang // tshegs chen yun ring rtogs pa'i phyir// lung bstan phyir mi ldog nyid dang // nges 'byung bar chad med bcas dang // byang chub nye dang myur ba dang // gzhan don 'phel
9b1(mdo 'grel): med 'grib med phyir// chos dang chos min sogs mi mthong // gzugs sogs bsam mi khyab mi mthong // gzugs sogs de yi mtshan ma dang // de yi ngo bo rnam mi rtog/ 'bras bu rin chen sbyin byed dang // de ni dag pa mtsham/
9b2(mdo 'grel): dang bcas// bdud kyi mthu bcom la sogs pa// yon tan rnam pa bcu bzhi'o// skyon ni bcu tshon bzhir bcas pa// drug tu nges par rtogs par bya// gang gis mtshon te mtshan nyid du// shes bya ba yang rnam pa gsum// shes
9b3(mdo 'grel): pa khyad par byed pa ste// ngo bo nyid gang mtshon bya yang // de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung ba dang // 'jig rten 'jig med bdag nyid dang // sems can sems kyi spyod pa dang // de bsdus pa dang phyir ltos dang // mi zad pa yi rnam pa
9b4(mdo 'grel): dang / chags bcas sogs dang rgya chen dang // chen por gyur dang tshad med dang // rnam shes bstan du med pa dang // sems bltar med dang shes pa de// g.yo ba la sogs shes bya dang // de las gzhan yang de dag ni// de bzhin nyid kyi
9b5(mdo 'grel): rnam par shes// thub pas de bzhin nyid rtogs te// gzhan la bstan pa zhes bya 'di// thams cad shes pa nyid skabs kyi// shes pa'i mtshan nyid bsdus pa yin// stong nyid mtshan ma med bcas dang // smon pa rnam par spangs pa dang // skye
9b6(mdo 'grel): med 'gag pa med sogs dang // chos nyid rnam par 'khrug med dang // 'du mi byed dang rnam mi rtog/ rab dbye mtshan nyid med nyid la// lam shes nyid kyi skabs kyis ni// shes pa'i mtshan nyid yin par bzhed// de ni nyid kyi chos bsten nas//
10a1(mdo 'grel): gnas dang gus par bya ba dang // bla ma nyid dang mnyes pa dang // de la mchod dang byed med dang // kun tu 'jug mkhyen gang yin dang // ma mthong ston par mdzad pa dang // 'jig rten stong nyid rnam pa dang // brjod dang
10a2(mdo 'grel): shes mdzad mngon sum mdzad// bsam mi khyab dang zhi nyid ston// 'jig rten 'du shes 'gog pa la// rnam pa kun mkhyen tshul la ni// shes pa'i mtshan nyid ces bshad do// bsam mi khyab sogs khyad par gyis// khyad zhugs bden
10a3(mdo 'grel): pa'i spyod yul can// skad cig ma ni bcu drug gis// khyad par mtshan nyid bshad pa yin// bsam mi khyab dang mi mnyam dang // gzhal dang bgrang las yang dag 'das// 'phags pa kun sdud mkhas pa yis// rig bya thun mong min
10a4(mdo 'grel): shes nyid// shes myur bri dang gang med dang // sgrub dang yang dag 'grub pa dang // dmigs pa rten dang bcas pa dang // mtha' dag pa dang yongs 'dzin dang // ro myang med dang khyad par ni// bcu drug bdag nyid ces bya ste// gang gis
10a5(mdo 'grel): lam ni gzhan dag las// khyad du 'phags pas khyad par lam// phan dang bde dang skyob pa dang // mi rnams kyi ni skyabs dag dang // gnas dang dpung gnyen gling dang ni// yongs 'dren pa zhes bya ba dang // lhun gyis grub dang theg gsum
10a6(mdo 'grel): gyi// 'bras bu mngon sum mi byed dag/ tha ma rten gyi mdzad pa ste// 'di ni byed pa'i mtshan nyid yin// nyon mongs rtags dang mtshan ma dang // mi mthun phyogs dang gnyen po dag/ dben dang dka' dang nges pa dang // tshad du bya dang mo
10b1(mdo 'grel): dmigs dang // mngon par zhen pa bkag pa dang // dmigs pa zhes bya gang yin dang // mi mthun thogs pa med dang de// gzhi med 'gro med skye med dang // de bzhin nyid ni mi dmigs dang // ngo bo nyid bcu drug bdag nyid// mtshon bya
10b2(mdo 'grel): lta bur mtshon pas na// mtshan nyid bzhi par bzhed pa yin// mtshan med rab tu sbyin la sogs// yang dag sgrub la mkhas pa ni// rnam pa thams cad rtogs 'di la// thar pa'i cha dang mthun par 'dod // sangs rgyas sogs dmigs dang
10b3(mdo 'grel): pa dang // sbyin sogs spyod yul brtson 'grus dang // bsam pa phun tshogs dran pa dang // rnam par mi rtog ting 'dzin dang // chos rnams rnam pa thams cad du// shes pa'i shes rab dang rnam lha// rdzogs pa'i byang chub rnon po yis//
10b4(mdo 'grel): rtogs bla rtul pos rtogs dkar bzhed// dro ba rnams kyi dmigs pa 'dir// sems can thams cad yin par bsngags// de dag nyid la sems mnyam sogs// rnam pa dag ni bcur bshad do// bdag nyid sdig pa las ldog cing //
10b5(mdo 'grel): sbyin la sogs la gnas pas gzhan// de dag la ni 'god pa dang // bsngags pa brjod dang mthun pa nyid// brtser gyur de bzhin bzod pa ni// rang gzhan rten can bden shes pa// chos mchog de bzhin sems can rnams// smin
10b6(mdo 'grel): byid sogs kyis shes par bya// nges 'byed yan lag nas bzung ste// mthong dang goms pa'i lam dag la// byang chub sems dpa' gang dag gnas// de 'dir phyir mi ldog pa'i tshogs// gzugs la sogs las ldog sogs
11a1(mdo 'grel): rtags// rnam pa nyi shur brjod pa yis// nges 'byed yan lag la gnas pa'i// phyir mi ldog pa'i mtshan nyid 'di// gzugs la sogs las ldog pa dang // the tshom mi dal zad pa dang // bdag nyid dge ba la gnas
11a2(mdo 'grel): shing // gzhan dag de la 'god pa dang // gzhan gyi rten can sbyin sogs dang // zab mo'i don la'ang som nyi med// byams lus sogs dang sgrib pa ni// rnam pa lnga dang mi 'grogs dang // bag la nyal kun 'joms pa dang // dran
11a3(mdo 'grel): pa dang ni shes bzhin dang // gos la sogs pa gtsang ba dang // lus la srin bu rnams mi 'byung // gya gyu med sems sbyangs pa ni// len dang ser sna med sogs dang // chos nyid ldan par 'gro nyid dang // sems can don du dmyal
11a4(mdo 'grel): chol dang // gzhan gyis bkri bar mi btub dang // lam gzhan nye bar ston bdud la// bdud ces bya bar rtogs pa dang // sangs rgyas dgyes pa'i spyod pa ste// rtags ni nyi shu de dag gis// drod dang rtse mo bzod bcas dang // chos
11a5(mdo 'grel): mchog rnams la gnas pa ni// rdzogs pa'i byang chub las mi ldog/ mthong ba'i lam la bzad pa dang // shes pa'i skad cig bcu drug ni// byang chub sems dpa' mi ldog pa'i// mtshan nyid yin par shes par bya// gzugs sogs 'du
11a6(mdo 'grel): shes ldog pa dang // sems brtan theg pa dman ngag las// rnam log bsam gtan la sogs pa'i// yan lag yongs su zad pa dang // lus sems yang ba nyid dang ni// 'dod la spyod la thabs mkhas dang // rtag tu tshangs par spyod
11b1(mdo 'grel): nyid dang // 'tsho ba rnam par dag nyid dang // phung sogs bar chad byed rnams dang // tshogs dang dbang sogs bcas pa yi// g.yul 'gyed ser sna la sogs la// sbyor dang rjes su sbyor ba yi// gnas pa so sor bkag pa dang // ches
11b2(mdo 'grel): ni rdul tsam mi dmigs nyid// rang gi sA la nges pa nyid// sa gsum la ni gnas pa dang // chos kyi don du srog gtong ba// de 'dra'i skad cig bcu drug ni// blo ldan mthong ba'i lam gnas kyi// phyir mi ldog pa'i rtag drag yin// sgom
11b3(mdo 'grel): pa'i lam ni zab pa ste// zab mo stong pa nyid la sogs// zab pa de ni sgro 'dogs dang // skur ba'i mtha' las grol ba nyid// nges 'byed yan lag dang mthong ba'i// lam dang sgom pa'i lam nyid la// yang dang yang du sems pa dang // 2ja
11b4(mdo 'grel): dang nges rtog sgom pa'i lam// de ni rgyun chags yin pa'i phyir// chung dang 'bring dang chen po rnams// chung ngu'i chung sogs dbye ba yis// rnam pas rnam pa dgur bzhed do// grangs med la sogs bstan pa rnams// dam pa'i don du bzod ma
11b5(mdo 'grel): yin/ kun rdzob tu ni thugs brtse ba'i// rgyu mthun de dag thob pa bzhad// dngos po brjod du med pa la// nyams pa dang ni 'phel mi rung // sgom zhes bya ba'i lam gyis ni// ci zhig nyams shing ci zhig 'thob// byang chub ji lta de bzhin du// 'di
11b6(mdo 'grel): ni 'dod po'i don sgrub byed// byang chub de bzhin nyid mtshan nyid// de yang de yi mtshan nyid bzhad// sems ni snga mas byang chub par// rigs min phyi mas kyang ni min// mar me'i dpe yi tshul gyis ni// zab mo'i chos nyid rnam pa brgyad// skye ba
12a1(mdo 'grel): dang ni 'gag pa dang // de bzhin nyid dang shes bya dang // shes dang spyod dang gnyis med dang // thabs mkhas pa la zab pa nyid// chos rnams rmi lam 'dra ba'i phyir// srid dang zhi bar mi rtogs pa// las med/
12a2(mdo 'grel): la sogs klan ka yi// lan ni ji skad bshad par zad// sems can 'jig rten de bzhin du// snod kyi 'jig rten ma dag pa// de la dag par sgrub pa yis// sangs rgyas zhing ni dag pa nyid// yul dang sbyor ba can 'di ni// dgra rnams
12a3(mdo 'grel): las ni 'das pa dang // mi gnas ji bzhin shugs dang ni// thun mong ma yin mtshan nyid dang // ma chags pa dang mi dmigs dang // mtshan ma smon lam zad pa dang // de yi rtags dang tshad med pa// thabs la mkhas pa rnam pa
12a4(mdo 'grel): bcu/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstun bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi tshig le'ur byas pa las/ skabs bzhi pa'o// // rmi lam na yang chos rnams kun// rmi lam lta bur lha la sogs// rtse mor
12a5(mdo 'grel): phyin pa'i sbyor ba'i rtags// rnam pa bcu gnyis dag tu bzhed// 'dzam bu'i gling gi skye bo snyed// sangs rgyas mchod pa'i dge la sogs// rnam mang du ni dper mdzad nas// rnam 'phel bcu drug bdag nyid do// kun mkhyen nyid gsum chos
12a6(mdo 'grel): rnams kyi// yongs su rdzogs pa bla med pa// sems can don yongs mi gtong ba// brtan pa zhes ni mngon par brjod// gling bzhi pa dang stong dag dang // stong gnyis gsum dag dper mdzad nas// bsod nams mang po nyid kyis ni// ting
12b1(mdo 'grel): 'dzin yongs su bsgrags pa sbyin// jug pa dang ni ldog pa la// gzung ba'i rnam rtags sor ro// dgu yi bdag nyid thabazhin yul// min pa'i bdag nyid dag shes bya/ sa mA rba skye bo 'phags dbye bsdu// snrums can rdzas dang
12b2(mdo 'grel): btags yod par// rnam rtog 'dzin pa dag tu 'dod// de dag so sor dgu bdag nyid// gal te gzung don de bzhin med// de dag gang gi 'dzin par 'dod// de ltar de dag 'dzin pa yi// je zla stong pa'i mtshan nyid do// ngo bo nyid dang rigs
12b3(mdo 'grel): dang ni// lam ni yang dag 'grub pa dang // shes pa'i dmigs pa ma 'khrul dang // mi mthun phyogs dang gnyen po dang // rang gi rtogs dang byed pa dang // de yi las bya'i 'bras bu la// 'jug pa'i phyogs kyi rten can gyi// rnam rtog de ni
12b4(mdo 'grel): rnam dgur 'dod// srid dang zhi bar ltung ba'i phyir// rtogs pa dman pa nyid dang ni// yongs su 'dzin pa med pa dang // lam gyi rnam pa ma tshang dang // gzhan gyi rkyen gyis 'gro ba dang // ched du bya ba log pa dang // nyi tshe ba dang sna tshogs nyid//
12b5(mdo 'grel): gnas dang 'jug la rmongs pa dang // rjes lo 'gro zhes bya ba la// rnam rtog dgu yi bdag nyid 'di// ldog pa'i phyogs kyi rten can te// nyan thos la sogs yid las 'byung // 'dzin pa dang ni 'dor ba dang // yid la byed dang khams rnams
12b6(mdo 'grel): gsum po dag dang khe 'brel dang // gnas dang mngon par zhen pa dang // chos kyi dngos po btags pa dang // chags pa dang ni gnyen po dang // ji ltar 'dod bzhin 'gro nyams la// 'dzin pa dang por shes par bya// ched bzhin nges par
13a1(mdo 'grel): mi 'byung dang // lam la lam min nges 'dzin dang // 'gog dang bcas pa'i skye ba dang // dngos po ldan dang mi ldan dang // gnas dang rigs ni 'jig pa dang // don du gnyer dang rgyu med dang // phyir rgol ba ni
13a2(mdo 'grel): dmigs pa la// 'dzin pa'i rnam rtog gzhan yin no// byang chub la gzhan ston pa dang // de yi rgyu ni yongs gtong dang // de thob par chad med pa'i rgyu// bsod nams mang po'i mtshan nyid do// dri ma zad dang mi skye ba'i// ye shes byang
13a3(mdo 'grel): chub ces brjod de// zad med skye mang phyir de dag/ go rim bzhin du shes par bya// 'gog pa med pa'i rang bzhin la// mthong zhes bya ba'i lam gyis ni// rnam par rtog rigs ci zhig zad // skye med rnam pa ci zhig 'thob// gzhan gyis chos
13a4(mdo 'grel): rnams kyang yod la// shes bya la yang ston pa yi// sgrib pa zad par brjod pa gang // de la kho bos mtshar du brtsis// 'di la bsal bya ci yang med// gzhag par bya ba cung zad med// yang dag nyid la yang dag lta// yang dag mthong nas rnam
13a5(mdo 'grel): par grol// sbyin pa la sogs re rer ni// de dag phan tshun bsdus pa gang // skad cig gcig pa'i bzod pa yis// bsdus pa de 'dir mthong ba'i lam// de nas seng ge rnam bsgyings pa'i// ting nge 'dzin la snyoms zhugs nas// rten cing
13a6(mdo 'grel): 'brel 'byung lugs mthun dang // lugs mi mthun la rtog par byed// 'gog dang bcas pa'i snyoms 'jug dgur// rnam pa gnyis su song 'ongs nas// 'dod par gtogs pa'i rnam par shes// mnyam gzhag min pa'i mtshams
13b1(mdo 'grel): bzung ste// thod rgal du ni snyoms 'jug pa// gcig dang gnyis gsum bzhi dang lnga// drug dang bdun dang brgyad brgal nas// 'gog pa'i bar du mi 'drar 'gro/ mdor bsdus rgyas dang sangs rgyas kyis// bstang bas yongs su ma bzung dang //
13b2(mdo 'grel): dus gsum yon tan med pa dang // legs pa'i lam ni rnam gsum la// gzung ba'i rnam rtog 'di gcig ste// sbyor ba'i rnam pa'i spyod yul can// gnyis pa sems dang sems byung rnams// 'jug pa'i yul can yin bzhed de// sems mi
13b3(mdo 'grel): skye dang byang chub kyi// snying po yid la mi byed dang // theg pa dman pa yid byed dang // rdzogs pa'i byang chub yid mi byed// sgom dang sgom pa med pa dang // de dag las ni bzlog nyid dang // ji bzhin don min rnam rtog pa// sgom pa'i lam la shes
13b4(mdo 'grel): par bya// sems can btags pa'i spyod yul dang // chos btags pa dang stong min nyid// chags dang rab 'byed bdag nyid dang // dngos por byed dang theg gsum dang // yon ni dag pa ma yin dang // spyod pa rnam par 'khrugs pa la// 'dzin par
13b5(mdo 'grel): byed pa dang por ste// shes par bya ba bsgrags pa yin// sems can btags dang de'i rgyu yi// yul can de yis rnams 'joms las// sgom pa'i lam dang 'brel pa yi// mi mthun phyogs gzhan rnam pa dgu// bdag nyid ji bzhin kun mkhyen
13b6(mdo 'grel): ni// gsum gyi sgrib pa rnam gsum dang // zhi lam de bzhin nyid sogs dang // mtshungs par ldan dang mi ldan dang // mi mnyam sdug bsngal la sogs dang // nyon mongs rnams kyi rang bzhin dang // gnyis su meng la kun rmongs la// rnam por
14a1(mdo 'grel): rtog pa tha mar bzhed// yams nang 'di rnams zad nas ni// yun ring lon nas dbugs phyin ltar// rnam pa kun tu 'gro ba yi// bde sgrub yon tan phun tshogs kun// rgya mtsho che la chu bo bzhin// 'bras
14a2(mdo 'grel): bu mchog gis spa ba yi// sems dpa' chen po de la ni// rnam pa kun tu rten par byed// stong gsum skye bo nyan thos dang // bse ru'i rtogs pa phun tshogs dang / byang chub sems dpa'i skyon med la// bkod pa'i dge ba dper mdzad
14a3(mdo 'grel): nas 'a bsod nams mang po nyid kyis ni// sangs rgyas nyid kyi bar med de// bar chad med pa'i ting nge 'dzin// de ni rnam pa kun mkhyen nyid// 'di yi dmigs pa dngos mod de// bdag po dran pa yin par bzhed// rnam pa zhi nyid 'di la ni// /
14a4(mdo 'grel): rab tu smra rnams rgyud mar rgol// dmigs pa 'thad dang de yi ni// ngo bo nyid nges bzung ba dang // rnam kun mkhyen nyid ye shes dang // dam pa'i don dang kun rdzob dang // sbyor dang dkon mchog gsum po dang // thabs bcas thub pa'i
14a5(mdo 'grel): rtogs pa dang // phyin ci log ni lam bcas dang // gnyen po mi mthun phyogs dag dang // mtshan nyid dang ni sgom pa la// smra ba rnams kyis log rtog pa// rnam pa kun mkhyen nyid rten can// rnam pa bcu drug dag tu bzhed// shes
14a6(mdo 'grel): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyun gyi tshig le'ur byas pa las/ skabs lnga pa 'o// / sbyin pa shes rab bar dag dang // sangs rgyas la sogs dran dang chos// dngos med

14b3(mdo 'grel): shes de bzhin mo// pa/ mas ste// hrI sna ba pa m+bu b+h+ya/ rnam sbyin nas smye sa smrangs skyes/ de gas mi gas/ sbyin sa zlog byung ba sa/ ma gan rdzu ma na/

15a1(mdo 'grel): mongs med dang sgron mkhyen dang // mngon shes so so yang dag rig/ rnam pa thams cad dag bzhi dang // dbang bcu dang ni stobs bcu dang // mi 'jigs pa ni bzhi dag dang // bsrung ba med pa rnam gsum dang // dran pa nyer
15a2(mdo 'grel): gzhag rnam gsum dang // bsnyel ba mi mnga'i chos nyid dang // bag chags yang dgra bcom pa dang // skye la thugs rje chen po dang // thub pa kho na'i ma 'dres chos// bco brgyad bshad pa gang yin dang // rnam pa thams cad mkhyen nyid dang // chos
15a3(mdo 'grel): kyi sku zhes brjod pa yin// nyan thos nyon mongs med pa'i lta// mi yi nyon mongs yongs spong nyid// grong sogs su de'i nyon mongs rnams// rgyun gcod rgyal ba'i nyon mongs med// sangs rgyas smon nas mkhyen pa ni// lhun gyis grub dang chags
15a4(mdo 'grel): spangs dang // thogs pa meng dang rtag gnas dang // dri ba kun lan 'debs par bzhed// rgyun yongs su smin gyur nas// gang dang gang la gang dang ni// gang tshe bya ba phan gyur pa// de dang de la de snang ngo // lha yi rgyal pos char phab kyang // sa bon mi
15a5(mdo 'grel): rung mi 'khrungs ltar// sangs rgyas rnams ni byung gyur kyang // skal ba med pas bzang mi myong // de ltar mdzad pa rgya che'i phyir// sangs rgyas khyab par nges par brjod// de nyid zad pa med pa'i phyir// rtag pa zhes kyang brjod pa yin// mtshan ni sum
15a6(mdo 'grel): cu rtsa gnyis dang // dpe byad brgyad cu'i bdag nyid 'di// theg chen nye bar longs spyod phyir// thub pa'i longs spyod rdzogs skur bzhed// phyag zhabs 'khor los mtshan dang ru sbal zhabs// phyag dang zhabs sor dra bas 'brel pa dang // phyag ni
15b1(mdo 'grel): zhabs bcas 'jam zhing gzhon sha chags// di yi sku ni bdun dag mtho ba dang // sor mo rang dang rting yangs sku che drang // zhabs 'bur mi mngon spya ni gyen du phyogs// byin pa a5'i 'dra phrug ring mdzes// 'doms kyi sba ba sbubs su nung/
15b2(mdo 'grel): pa'i mchog/ pags pa gser mdog pags pa srab pa dang // spu ni re re nas g.yas legs 'khrungs dang // zhal mdzod spus rgyan ro stod seng ge'i 'dra// 'di yi dpung pa'i mgo zlum thal gong rgyas// 'di la ri mo zhim pa ro mchog snang //
15b3(mdo 'grel): sku ni n+ya gro d+ha ltar chu zheng gab// gtsug tor dbur ldan ljags ring mdzes pa dang // tshangs dbyangs 'gram pa seng ge'i 'dra dang tshams// shin tu dkar dang tshad mnyam thags bzang dang // grangs ni bzhi bcu tham par tshang ba dang // spyan ni mthon
15b4(mdo 'grel): mthong spyan rdzib mchog gi/ 'dra ba 'di dag sum cu rtsa gnyis mtshan// 'di la mtshan ni gang gang gi/ sgrub par byed pa'i rgyu gang yin// de dang de ni rab rdzogs pas// mtshan ni 'di dag yang dag 'grub// bla ma skyel la sogs pa dang // yang
15b5(mdo 'grel): dag blangs pa brtan pa dang // b+hasdu ba bsten dang gyu nom pa'i// dngos po sbyin dang bsad bya ba// thar par byed dang dge ba ni// yang dag blangs pa spel la sogs// sgrub byed rgyu yi mtshan nyid de// mdo las ji skad 'byung ba bzhin// thub pa'i sen mo
15b6(mdo 'grel): zings mdog dang / mdog snum maSh+To dang sor mi rnams// zlum rgyas byin gyis phru bo dang // rtsa mi mngon dang mdud pa med// long bu mi mngon zhabs mnyam dang // seng ge glang chen bya dang ni// khyu mchog stabs gshegs g.yas phyogs
16a1(mdo 'grel): dang // mdzes klu shegs drang dang 'khril bag chags// byi dor byas 'dra rim par 'tsham// gcad dang 'ang ma dang dag pa'i sku// mtshan ni yongs su rdzogs pa dang // sku y-i kho lag yangs shing
16a2(mdo 'grel): bzang / gom snyoms pa dang spyan gnyis ni// ngag dang gzhon sha can nyid dang // sku zhum med dang rgyas pa dang // shin tu grims pa'i sku nyid dang // yan lag shin tu rnam 'byes dang // gzigs pa sgrib med dag pa dang // dgra
16a3(mdo 'grel): zlum skabs phyin ma rnyongs dang // phyang nge ba dang lte ba ni// zab dang g.yas phyogs 'khyil ba dang // kun nas lta na sdug pa dang // kun spyod gtsang dang sku la ni// sme ba gnag bag med pa dang // phyag ni shing bal ltar 'jam dang //
16a4(mdo 'grel): phyog ris mdangs yod zab ring dang // zhal ni ha cang mi ring dang // mchu ni bim+ba ltar dmar dang // ljags mnyen pa dang srab pa dang // dmyor dang 'brug gi sgra nyid dang // gsung mnyen 'jam dang mche ba zlum// rno dang dkar dang mnyam
16a5(mdo 'grel): pa dang // byin gyis phra dang shangs mtho dang // mchog tu dag pa dag dang ni// spyan yangs pa dang rdzi ma sdug/ pad+ma'i 'dab ma 'dra ba dang // smin tshugs ring dang 'jam pa dang / snum dang spu ni mnyam pa dang // phyag ring rgyas dang snyan
16a6(mdo 'grel): mnyam dang // nyams pa rnam par spangs pa dang // dpral ba legs par 'byes pa dang // dbyes che ba deng dbu rgyas dang // dgu skra bung ba ltar gnag dang // sdug dang 'jam dang mi 'dzings dang / mi bshor dri zhim skyes bu yi// yid
16b1(mdo 'grel): ni 'phrog par byed pa dang // dngul gyi be'u dang bkra shis ni// g.yung drung 'khyil pas brgyan pa ste// sangs rgyas dpe byad bzang por bzhed// gang gis srid pa ji snyed par// 'gro la phan pa sna tshogs dag/ mnyam du mdzad pa'i sku
16b2(mdo 'grel): de ni// thub pa'i sprul sku rgyun mi 'chad// de bzhin 'khor ba ji srid 'di'o// las ni rgyun mi 'chad par 'dod// 'gro rnams zhi ba'i las dang ni// bsdu rnam bzhi la dgod pa dang // kun nas nyon mongs bcas pa yi// rnam par byang ba
16b3(mdo 'grel): rtogs pa dang / sems can rnams don ji bzhin gyi// don dang pha rol phyin drug dang // sangs rgyas lam dang rang bzhin gyis// stong pa nyid dang gnyis zad dang // brda dang dmigs pa med pa dang // lus can rnams ni yo
16b4(mdo 'grel): smin dang // byang chub sems dpa'i lam dang ni// mngon par zhen pa bzlog pa dang // byang chub thob dang sangs rgyas zhing // rnam par dag dang nges pa dang // sems can don ni tshad med dang // sangs rgyas rten sogs yon tan
16b5(mdo 'grel): dang / byang chub yan lag las rnams ni// chung mi za dang bden mthong dang // phyin ci log ni spangs pa dang // de gzhi med pa'i tshul dang ni// rnam par byang dang tshegs dang ni// 'dus byas 'dus ma byas pA la// tha dad yongs su
16b6(mdo 'grel): mi shes dang // mya ngan 'das la dgod pa ste// chos kyi sku yi phrin las ni// rnam pa nyi shu bdun du bzhed/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi tshig le'ur byas pa las//
17a1(mdo 'grel): skabs brgyad pa'o// / mtshan nyid de yi sbyor ba dang // de rab de yi go rim dang // de mtha' de yi rnam smin ni// don bsdus gzhan de rnam pa drug/ yul ni rnam pa gsum rgyu/
17a2(mdo 'grel): sbyor ba bzhi yi bdag nyid dang // chos sku phrin las 'bras bu ni// ngan bsdus gzhan te rnam pa gsum// 'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan zhes bya ba'i tshig le
17a3(mdo 'grel): byobyis pa rdzogs so// / paN+Di ta go mi 'chi med dang / lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur//
18a1(mdo 'grel): 'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa stong phrag nyi shu lnga pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi 'grel pa nyi khri snang ba bzhugs//
18b1(mdo 'grel): rgya gar skad du/ pany+tsa bidra ti sa ha sri ka Ar+ya pradz+nyA pa ra mi to pa de shA b+hi sa ma yA laM kA ra shAs+t+ra s+ya pret+ti/ bod skad du/ 'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa stong phrag nyi shu lnga pa'i man ngag gi bstan
18b2(mdo 'grel): bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi 'grel pa/ bcom ldan 'das yum shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma la phyag 'tshal lo// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo// nyan thos zhi
18b3(mdo 'grel): ba tshol rnams kun shes nyid kyis nyer zhir khrid mdzad gang yin dang // 'gro la phan par byed rnams lam shes nyid kyis 'jig rten don sgrub mdzad pa gang // gang dang yang dag ldan pas thub rnams rnam pa kun ldan sna tshogs 'di gsung
18b4(mdo 'grel): ba/ nyan thos byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs bcas sangs rgyas kyi ni yum de la phyag 'tshalo// don gang zhig yin zhe na/ 'phags pa'i gang zag thams cad kyi dbang du mdzad nas thams cad mkhyen pa rnam pa gsum gyi thun mong ma yin
18b5(mdo 'grel): pa'i yon tan nye bar dgod pa sngon du 'gro bas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la phyag 'tshal lo// zhes brjod pa 'di ni de'i mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi man ngag bshad sbyar du bya'o snyam pas rnam par dgrol bar bya'o// zhes mngon par
18b6(mdo 'grel): rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi bshad pa 'di sbyar bar dam bcas pa yin no// ci'i don du zhe na/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen nyid lam// ston pas 'di las bshad pa gang // gzhon gyis myong ba ma yin te// chos spyod bcu yi bdag nyid kyi// mdo
19a1(mdo 'grel): don dran pa la bzhag nas// blo dang ldan pas mthong 'gyur phyir// bde blag tu ni rtogs pa zhes// bya ba rtsom pa'i dgos pa yin// zhes de ltar phyag 'tshal ba nye bar bkod pa'i tshogs su bcad par yang dag par mtshon
19a2(mdo 'grel): pa'i don 'di yod pa yin no// zhes gsungs pa yin no// ci mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan 'di gzhi bsdus pas sam/ 'on te gnyen po bsdus pas sam/ de ste rnam pa bsdus pas brgyan du byed pa yin zhes brjod par bya ba yin no// de
19a3(mdo 'grel): las kyang cir 'gyur zhe na/ phyogs dang po ltar na ni 'bad pa don du med pa yin te/ mdo sde 'di las mtshan nyid kyi bstan bcos dag las mi smos pa'i gzhi gang yin pa de bshad pa ni med do// gnyis pa ltar na rnam par byang ba'i
19a4(mdo 'grel): dngos po bsdus pa'i phyir kun nas nyon mongs pa'i dngos po ma bsdus pas 'di gang gi gnyen po yin pa rtogs par mi 'gyur ro// gsum pa ltar na yang rnam pa gzhi med pa tsam zhig bsdus pa'i phyir/ don rtogs pa med pas cung
19a5(mdo 'grel): zad kyang ma bshad pa yin no zhe na/ phyogs gsum char gyis kyang bsdus pa yin no// zhes gsungs pa yin no// ci'i phyir zhe na/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' dang / sangs rgyas rnams kyi rim pa ji
19a6(mdo 'grel): lta ba bzhin thams cad shes pa nyid dang / lam shes pa nyid dang / rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyis mngon par rtogs pa mtha' dag bsdus pa'i phyir ro// ji skod du bcom ldan 'das kyis rab 'byor thams cad shes pa
19b1(mdo 'grel): nyid ni/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas rnams kyi yin no// lam shes pa nyid ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yin no// rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs
19b2(mdo 'grel): rgyas rnams kyi yin no// bcom ldan 'das ci'i slad du thams cad 'tshal ba nyid nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas rnams kyi lags/ rab 'byor thams cad ni phyi dang nang gi chos rnams ji snyed pa 'di tsam yin la de dag nyan thos
19b3(mdo 'grel): dang / rang sangs rgyas rnams kyis shes kyi/ lam thams cad kyis kyang ma yin la/ rnam pa thams cad du'ang ma yin pas de'i phyir nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas rnams kyi ni thams cad shes pa nyid ces bya'o// bcom ldan 'das
19b4(mdo 'grel): ci'i slad du lam gyi rnam pa 'tshal ba nyid/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lags/ rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis ni/ nyan thos kyi lam gang yin pa dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi lam gang yin pa dang / sangs
19b5(mdo 'grel): rgyas kyi lam gang yin pa'i lam thams cod bskyed par bya zhing lam thams cad shes par byo la/ de dag kyang yongs su rdzogs par bya zhing / de dag gis lam gyi bya ba yang bya ste/ smon lam yongs su rdzogs par ma byas
19b6(mdo 'grel): nga / sems can rnams yongs su smin par ma byas pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su ma sbyangs pa de dag gis/ yang dag pa'i mtha' mngon sum du mi bya'o// de'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ni lam ni rnam
20a1(mdo 'grel): par shes pa nyid ces bya'o// bcom ldan 'das ci'i slad du/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi lags/ rab 'gyur
20a2(mdo 'grel): rnam pa gang dag dang / rtags gang dag dang / mtshan ma gang dag gis chos rnams rab tu mtshon pa'i rnam pa de dag dang / rtags de dag dang / mtshan ma de dag de bzhin gshegs pas thugs su chud de/ de'i phyir de bzhin
20a3(mdo 'grel): gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi ni/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid ces bya'o// zhes gsungs pa yin no// de la thams cad shes pa nyid ni chos la 'bad pa'i rten can 'bras bu
20a4(mdo 'grel): bdag tu rmongs pa spangs pa can yin no// lam shes pa nyid ni theg pa ji lta ba bzhin du nges par 'byung ba dang / de kho na nyid mngon sum du mi byed pa'i rten can/ sems can bsdus pa sdud pa dang / sems can yongs su ma
20a5(mdo 'grel): smin pa yongs su smin par byed pa dang / sems can yongs su smin pa rnam par grol bar byed pa'i 'bras bu can yin no// rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid ni/ nam mkha'i khams kyi mthas gtugs par sems can gyi
20a6(mdo 'grel): don rgyun mi 'chad pa dang / yong dag pa'i mtha' rtogs pa dang / bag chags kyi mtshams sbyor ba spangs pa'i 'bras bu can yin no// de lta bas na mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan ni gzhi dang gnyen po dang / rnam pa rnams bsdus pas
20b1(mdo 'grel): mngon par rtogs pa yongs su rdzogs par mtha' dag bstan pa yin no// zhes bya ba 'di 'brang ba yin no// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa de gang yin zhes bya ba 'di ni brjod par byaHzhan bshad ba shes rab pha rol phyin pa ni//
